 Since the inception of Test cricket in the year 1877, many changes have been made in its rules
 test cricket badlaav ke ek or muhane par he
 On 27 November 2015 it is entering day-night cricket
 iske saath hi isamen pink ball ke prayog kii parampara bhi shuru hogi
 For the first time Day Night cricket will be played on the same pitch for five consecutive days
 isamen jahaan ek ore pich ke vyavhaar par najar rahegi vahiin duusari pink ball sabase adhik charchaa kaa vishay bana hua he kyonki iskaa prayog bhi pehali baar hi kiya ja rahaa he or iske vyavhaar ko lekar puure cricket jagat main utsukata bani hui he
 White in odis, why not in Tests? In odis, a white ball is used for 25 overs only
 isamen donon hi chor se nai genden prayog main laai jaati hai
 The reason behind this is, the color of the white ball does not deteriorate quickly and it can be seen easily in milky light
 vahiin test cricket main lagaataar 80 overs kaa match hone ke baad hi gend badalane kaa niyam he
 Only after one innings of one-day innings, the color of the white ball starts turning brown, while its color will become dark brown by 80 overs
 bhuri pich hoti he
 That is, not only the batsmen but also the fielders will get a lot of trouble from this
 iske saath hi test bhale hi de nite ho rahaa he cricketrs kii poshaak kaa rang safed hi rahegaa
 That is, there is no question of playing this test with white ball
 kaise pink ball kaa hua chayan?laal rang kii gend ke saath bhi safed rang kii tarah hi badi samasya he
 Traditional Test cricket is played in the light of day with a red ball
 lekin jab yahi gend dudhia raushnee main dekhi jaae to bhura dikhti he
 Which is also the color of the pitch
 isi vajah se de nite cricket ke liye ise pehle hi khaarij kar diya gaya tha
 The steady decline in viewership to watch Test cricket prompted the experts for this experiment
 iske liye sabase pehle jaruri tha gend kaa chayan
 Experts at MCC wanted to have the maximum similarity in quality and behavior between the two balls (red and the ball that was selected for the day night test)
 yani dudhia raushnee main insaani ankhon ko dekhne main koi pareshaani nahin ho
 After intense study, the Imperial College of London experts preferred pink over all other colors
 export ne pink main bhi 15 vibhinn shed par prayog kiya
 Eventually the pink colored ball to be used in this historic test was preferred
 pink kaise alag he test kii laal gend se?pink, laal or safed teenon hi gendon main adhiktam samanta he
 There is no difference in the bounce, stiffness and leather of these balls
 haa, pink main rangon ke alaava ek khaas antar he
 Actually, another layer of pink ballper color is added during finishing
 isaki vajah se ball kaa rang kuch adhik antaraal tak chamkila bana rahaa he or lambey samay tak khilne kii avasthaa main bana rahata he
 Coloring the ball was not very difficult for experts
 bat or ball ke bich kis prakaar santulan bana rahegaa? yah unke liye sabase badi chunauti thi
 It was important for them to know how it would behave when used in a ball match
 How will it bounce? How will it behave when the appearance of the ball deteriorates after use? All these aspects were considered in finalizing the pink ball

 udaipur sthit narayan seva santhaan ke varisht sarjan dow

 aap unase baat kiijie

 unki pidaa ko baahar laaiye
 Our colleague Sohit Mishra also visited these students a day before Holi
 din bhar unke saath bhatakate rahe

 sohit chaahate hai ki aap darshak dekhen ki aapke noujvaan kis mushkil sthiti main rahakar taiyaari karte hai or inke saath sarkarein kis tarah se dhokhaa karti hai
 After all, why the government is not providing jobs, if it is not to be given, then it will be clear that we will not give it, but what is the reason for hanging the qualification examinations by hanging out for many years
 sohit mishra kaa dhanyavad jo holi ke ek din pehle bhi zaruri story lekar aa gaye, aamtaur par is din channelon ke reporter kisi gayak ko khoj rahe hote hai jo holi par ga de, jise lekar tivi kaa spes bharaa ja sake
 Sohit has sent a story from Mumbai to fill this space with empty aspirations of an empty stomach
 kisi bhi rajya kaa chayan ayog ho, isane hamaare naujavaanon ko rula diya he

 chaar-chaar saal tak pariksha kaa chakra puraa nahin hota he

 hamen yakeen nahin hua or na hi ham isaki pushti kar sake

 The cycle of examination is not completed for four years
 hamaari naukari series esayssi ke kaaran shuru hui thi
 From August to October 2017, the results of about 15,000 youngsters were reported
 merit list main naam aane ke baad chuppi pasar gai

 prakriya kab shuru hogi
 Troubled, the youth started calling but still no answer
 chaatro ne bataaya ki hamen niyukti patr nahin milegaa, kyonki 12 janvari ko ek aadesh niklaa he ki niyukti kii prakriya roak di jaae
 We could not believe it nor could we confirm it
 tabhi 29 janvari ko sanchaar mantralay se ek chitthee jari hoti he
 Its first line states that on 12 January the order of the Director of the Postal Department was that all circles should be stopped from the appointment of those who passed the SSC 2015 examination, till further orders
 chaatro kii 12 janvari vaale aadesh kii baat sahi thi
 In this order, it had come out that now the order has been issued that the process of appointment of 5205 youths of the Postal Department should be started
 jab ham yah series shuru kar rahe the tab sieji main jin chaatro kaa hua tha wo khub messej bhej rahe the
 Was calling tang kar diya tha
 He said that no one is talking to the CAG
 hamen kaaphi hairaani hui
 Vinod Rai is unable to speak, but the CAG can only speak after him
 pataa chalaa ki alag-alag padon ke kareeb 1700 naujavaanon kii naukari kaa sawaal vahaan atka padaa he
 During our series, the CAG had to speak for the first time that SSC has sent their dossiers
 isamen certificate, paas hone kaa pramaan patr vagairah hota he
 The result was arrived in August 2017, the dossier had not arrived for six months
 ye haal he esayssi kaa
 But after that again silence
 ham bich-bich main sieji kaa zikr karte rahe
 But on March 1, there is double good news
 kareeb 700 chaatro kii jwining kaa notification sieji kii site par aa gaya he
 The first news reported that 200 auditors have been allocated to the state CAG
 rajya mukhyalayon se ab niyukti patr milanaa shuru ho jayega
 By evening, another news came that 500 accountants have also been divided among the states
 rajyon ko inkaa dosier bheja ja rahaa, taaki niyukti patr jari ho sake
 The comments is series ke dauraan sieji ke chayaraman ne apni website par ek notification jari kiya, jisamen meri taraf ishaara kiya gaya ki ek channel buree niyat se yah sab kaam kar rahaa he
 My intention was not bad, i was sure that this series would go on until they get the letter
 esayssi ke chairman asheem khurana ji ne ek or patr website par daalaa ki inaki niyukti main esayssi kii koi bhoomika nahin he, enditivi ke ankar ko is sthiti kii jaankaree nahin he
 Now it is written in all the orders that SSC has sent the dossiers of the students, the process of recruitment is starting
 8 se 9 hazaar chaatro kii niyukti kii prakriya shuru ho gai he
 You can ask those young people about this series
 uske pehle kitne hataash the, ab kitni aashaaon or umangon se bhare hai
 They have blossomed like the colors of Holi
 ummid kii jaani chahie ki hamaari naukari series ke baad chayan ayog sudharenge

 avaidh coloniyon ke maamle par mukhyamantri tej barish ke bich hi kendriya shahari vikaas mantri se milane pahunchi

 karthik maas main radha-damodar ke saath shaligram tathaa tulsi ke pujan kaa vishesh mahatv he
 According to religious scriptures, the Supindi Shraddha is very important on the day of Kartik Shukla Chaturdashi
 is din pitaron ke nimitt sidghwat va ramghat par supindi shraadh daan kiya jaataa he
 On this day especially, it is a law to donate tarpan, donation and body for the peace and prosperity of ancestors' soul
 kya karen karthik chaturdashi ke din:* nirnay sindhu kii manyata ke anusaar karthik chaturdashi par sarvapratham tirth snaan karen
 * After worshiping radha-damodar or shaligram-tulsi, perform Tarapan and Supindi Shraddha for the ancestors
 * radha-damodar kaa pujan suhaagin striyon ke liye chir saubhagyadaayak hota he
 * tulsi-shaligram is worshiped for happiness, peace, prosperity in the family
 * radha-damodar, shaligram tathaa tulsi tathaa bhagwaan kartikeya kaa pujan karen
 * Performing tarpan and supindi shraddha for ancestors is considered to attain happiness and advance higher lineage
 * is din purvamukhi hokar srihari va har yani shiv ji kaa pujan karnaa chahie
 * Add saffron to cow ghee (cow's ghee) and light a lamp, worship it with sandalwood incense sticks and offer saffron
 * srihari ko camel kaa pushp chadhaane se ve prasann hote hai at: pujan ke samay camel pushp arpit karen or makhane kii kheer kaa bhoga lagaaein
 * Offer prasad to the cow after worship
